    var anjuke_web_global_InitTracker=function(city_id,city_cookie_name,guid_cookie_name,base_domain,cookie_path){
        var expire=365*5;
        var guid=this.getCookie(guid_cookie_name);
        if(null==guid){
            guid=this.createGuid();this.setCookie(guid_cookie_name,guid,expire,cookie_path,base_domain);
        }else{
            this.setCookie(guid_cookie_name,guid,expire+1,cookie_path,base_domain);
        }
        if(city_id!=this.getCookie(city_cookie_name)){
            this.setCookie(city_cookie_name,city_id,expire,cookie_path,base_domain);
        }
        var session_cookie_name='sessid';var session_id=this.getCookie(session_cookie_name);if(null==session_id){
            session_id=this.createGuid();this.setCookie(session_cookie_name,session_id,0,cookie_path,base_domain);
        }
        this.setCookie('isp', 'true', expire, cookie_path, base_domain);
    };anjuke_web_global_InitTracker.prototype.createGuid=function(){
        return(this.S4()+this.S4()+"-"+this.S4()+"-"+this.S4()+"-"+this.S4()+"-"+this.S4()+this.S4()+this.S4());
    };anjuke_web_global_InitTracker.prototype.S4=function(){
        return(((1+Math.random())*0x10000)|0).toString(16).substring(1).toUpperCase();
    };anjuke_web_global_InitTracker.prototype.getCookie=function(check_name){
        var a_all_cookies=document.cookie.split(';');var a_temp_cookie='';var cookie_name='';var cookie_value='';var b_cookie_found=false;for(i=0;i<a_all_cookies.length;i++){
            a_temp_cookie=a_all_cookies[i].split('=');cookie_name=a_temp_cookie[0].replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,'');if(cookie_name==check_name){
                b_cookie_found=true;if(a_temp_cookie.length>1){
                    cookie_value=unescape(a_temp_cookie[1].replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,''));
                }
                return cookie_value;break;
            }
            a_temp_cookie=null;cookie_name='';
        }
        if(!b_cookie_found){
            return null;
        }
    };anjuke_web_global_InitTracker.prototype.setCookie=function(name,value,expires,path,domain,secure){
        var today=new Date();today.setTime(today.getTime());if(expires){
            expires=expires*1000*60*60*24;
        }
        var expires_date=new Date(today.getTime()+(expires));document.cookie=name+"="+escape(value)+
            ((expires)?";expires="+expires_date.toGMTString():"")+
            ((path)?";path="+path:"")+
            ((domain)?";domain="+domain:"")+
            ((secure)?";secure":"");
    };
